                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Just in time for your annual New Year’s resolution to get in better shape, Under Armour and HTC have debuted a new all-in-one, connected fitness-tracking system." data-reactid="27">Just in time for your annual New Year’s resolution to get in better shape, Under Armour and HTC have debuted a new all-in-one, connected fitness-tracking system.</p>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Called the UA HealthBox and designed with HTC, the $400 system comes with a fitness tracker, a connected scale, and a heart-rate monitor, which all feed information into a smartphone app to give you a better understanding of your overall health." data-reactid="28">Called the UA HealthBox and designed with HTC, the $400 system comes with a fitness tracker, a connected scale, and a heart-rate monitor, which all feed information into a smartphone app to give you a better understanding of your overall health.</p>

                   <h2 class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="UA Record app" data-reactid="66">UA Record app</h2>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="The crux of the UA HealthBox system is Under Armour’s <a href=&quot;https://record.underarmour.com/&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>UA Record app</a> for Android and iOS. It pulls in data from the fitness tracker, scale, and heart-rate monitor, then breaks it down into four categories: Activity, Fitness, Nutrition, and Sleep.</p>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<b><i>Related: More coverage of <a href=&quot;https://www.yahoo.com/tech/tagged/CES-2016&quot;>CES 2016</a>.</i></b>" data-reactid="68"><b><i>Related: More coverage of <a href="https://www.yahoo.com/tech/tagged/CES-2016">CES 2016</a>.</i></b></p>
